cd octagons/tests; \
	rm -rf klee-out-* ; \
	clang -I /home/klee/klee_src/include -I ../ -I ../../num -I ../../apron -emit-llvm -O0 -c -g *.c -g -DNUM_LONGDOUBLE; \
        number=0 ; while [ ${number} -le 9 ] ; do \
		llvm-link ../*.bc ../../apron/*.bc test_oct.bc test_oct${number}.bc -o test${number}.bc ; \
		startTime=`date +%s` ; \
                klee -allow-external-sym-calls -sym-malloc-bound=8192 -max-forks=100 -solver-backend=stp test${number}.bc ; \
		endTime=`date +%s` ; \
                runtime=`expr $endTime - $startTime` ; \
                echo "Execution time: $runtime sec for test_oct$number\n" ; \
		number=`expr $number + 1` ; \
    	done; \
        true

Execution time: 487 sec for test_oct9

cd octagons/tests; \
	rm -rf klee-out-* ; \
	clang -I /home/klee/klee_src/include -I ../ -I ../../num -I ../../apron -emit-llvm -O0 -c -g *.c -g -DNUM_LONGDOUBLE; \
        number=10 ; while [ ${number} -le 19 ] ; do \
		llvm-link ../*.bc ../../apron/*.bc test_oct.bc test_oct${number}.bc -o test${number}.bc ; \
		startTime=`date +%s` ; \
                klee -allow-external-sym-calls -sym-malloc-bound=8192 -max-forks=100 -solver-backend=stp test${number}.bc ; \
		endTime=`date +%s` ; \
                runtime=`expr $endTime - $startTime` ; \
                echo "Execution time: $runtime sec for test_oct$number\n" ; \
		number=`expr $number + 1` ; \
    	done; \
        true

cd octagons/tests; \
	rm -rf klee-out-* ; \
	clang -I /home/klee/klee_src/include -I ../ -I ../../num -I ../../apron -emit-llvm -O0 -c -g *.c -g -DNUM_LONGDOUBLE; \
        number=20 ; while [ ${number} -le 29 ] ; do \
		llvm-link ../*.bc ../../apron/*.bc test_oct.bc test_oct${number}.bc -o test${number}.bc ; \
		startTime=`date +%s` ; \
                klee -allow-external-sym-calls -sym-malloc-bound=8192 -max-forks=100 -solver-backend=stp test${number}.bc ; \
		endTime=`date +%s` ; \
                runtime=`expr $endTime - $startTime` ; \
                echo "Execution time: $runtime sec for test_oct$number\n" ; \
		number=`expr $number + 1` ; \
    	done; \
        true

cd octagons/tests; \
	rm -rf klee-out-* ; \
	clang -I /home/klee/klee_src/include -I ../ -I ../../num -I ../../apron -emit-llvm -O0 -c -g *.c -g -DNUM_LONGDOUBLE; \
        number=30 ; while [ ${number} -le 39 ] ; do \
		llvm-link ../*.bc ../../apron/*.bc test_oct.bc test_oct${number}.bc -o test${number}.bc ; \
		startTime=`date +%s` ; \
                klee -allow-external-sym-calls -sym-malloc-bound=8192 -max-forks=100 -solver-backend=stp test${number}.bc ; \
		endTime=`date +%s` ; \
                runtime=`expr $endTime - $startTime` ; \
                echo "Execution time: $runtime sec for test_oct$number\n" ; \
		number=`expr $number + 1` ; \
    	done; \
        true
